class="markdown-body markdown-custom-styles"><h1>Privacy Policy</h1>
<p><strong>Effective as of 2024-02-05</strong></p>
<p><strong>similarGPTs.com</strong> (“we,” “our,” or “us”) is dedicated to safeguarding your privacy. This Privacy Policy outlines how we handle your personal information.</p>
<p>This Privacy Policy applies to our website and its associated subdomains (collectively, our “Service”) as well as our application, similarGPTs.com. By accessing or using our Service, you acknowledge that you have read, understood, and agree to the collection, storage, use, and disclosure of your personal information as detailed in this Privacy Policy and our Terms of Service.</p>
<h2>Definitions and Key Terms</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Cookie:</strong> A small piece of data stored by your web browser to remember information about you.</li>
<li><strong>Company:</strong> When this policy mentions “Company,” “we,” “us,” or “our,” it refers to similarGPTs.com.</li>
<li><strong>Country:</strong> The country where similarGPTs.com or its owners are based, in this case, USA.</li>
<li><strong>Customer:</strong> Refers to companies, organizations, or individuals that use the similarGPTs.com Service.</li>
<li><strong>Device:</strong> Any internet-connected device like a phone, tablet, or computer.</li>
<li><strong>IP address:</strong> A number assigned to a device on the Internet for identification purposes.</li>
<li><strong>Personal Data:</strong> Information that can be used to identify a person.</li>
<li><strong>Service:</strong> The service provided by similarGPTs.com as described on this platform.</li>
<li><strong>Third-party service:</strong> External companies or services that we partner with or utilize.</li>
<li><strong>Website:</strong> The similarGPTs.com site, accessible via https://similargpts.com/.</li>
<li><strong>You:</strong> A person or entity registered with similarGPTs.com to use the Services.</li>
</ul>
<h2>How Do We Use The Information?</h2>
<p>The collected information may be used to personalize your experience, improve our website and customer service, process transactions, administer contests or promotions, send periodic emails, and for other similar purposes.</p>
<h2>Collection of Information from Third Parties</h2>
<p>We may collect information from third parties, including when you use social media to interact with our service, and from other third-party sources that are lawfully entitled to share your data with us.</p>
<h2>Sharing Information with Third Parties</h2>
<p>We may share your information with advertisers, promotional partners, affiliates, and other third parties for business purposes and as legally required.</p>
<h2>Security of Your Information</h2>
<p>We take various measures to ensure the security of your personal data, including the use of SSL technology for transactions and restricted access to your data by authorized personnel.</p>
<h2>International Data Transfers</h2>
<p>Your information may be transferred and stored in different countries, including those without the same data protection laws as your jurisdiction.</p>
<h2>Your Rights and Choices</h2>
<p>You have the right to access, update, delete, or restrict the use of your personal data. We provide mechanisms for updating your data and managing your communication preferences.</p>
<h2>Changes to the Privacy Policy</h2>
<p>We may update this policy to reflect changes to our practices or for other operational, legal, or regulatory reasons.</p>
<h2>Contact Us</h2>
<p>For any questions about this Privacy Policy, please contact us via <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__"
